            <section class="page-section" id="about">
        <h2 class="visually-hidden">About Modules</h2>
        <div class="container">
          <div class="page-section__text">
                                      <p class="fib page-section__link" data-animate="">Modules is a project by <a href="https://zhestkov.studio/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer">Maxim Zhestkov</a>, where different forms of art – architecture, sculpture, film, and music – blend together to create an intense, interactive virtual experience.</p>
<p class="fib page-section__link" data-animate="">A total work of art by Zhestkov, it is a world that questions the established definitions of our reality. In digital space, we can abandon the logic of reality and are freed from its boundaries. New worlds with total freedom are possible, worlds only limited by our creativity and the potential of art.</p>
                      </div>
          <div class="page-section__content">
            <div class="get-apps page-section__get-apps fib" data-animate="">

              new territories and blurring the boundaries between art, games, and reality.</p>

              projects&nbsp;— Modul, released in&nbsp;2009. Reimagined as&nbsp;a&nbsp;series of&nbsp;surreal
              experiences with space and dynamic sculptures, Modules is&nbsp;an&nbsp;immersive experience that can
              be&nbsp;seen both in&nbsp;VR headset and on&nbsp;a&nbsp;desktop.</p>

  const value = this.value.trim()
  if (value !== '' && value.indexOf('http') !== 0) {
    this.value = 'http://' + value
  }
}
